             SEPARATION OF INSUREDS AND ADDITIONAL INSURED OPERATION
_________________________________________________________________________________________________
THIS FORM IS PART OF THE POLICY AND MUST BE READ WITH THE DECLARATIONS AND ENDORSEMENTS.


The commercial general liability contract clearly distinguishes      To secure protection for liabilities arising after project
between the primary named insured and other parties who may          completion, a specific completed operations additional insured
receive incidental protection.                                       endorsement must be attached.

The named insured is the entity explicitly listed on the             Primary and non-contributory conditions are frequently
declarations page and bears the primary administrative               requested by external parties seeking additional insured status
responsibilities for the contract.                                   on the contract.

These administrative duties include the payment of all               When this condition is properly endorsed, the protection
premiums, the reporting of operational changes, and the              provided by this contract will respond before any other
maintenance of accurate exposure records.                            insurance available to the additional insured.

Additional insureds are external individuals or organizations       We will not seek contribution from the additional insured own
granted specific, limited protection through the attachment of a     liability policies if the primary and non-contributory requirement
designated endorsement.                                              is met.

The protection afforded to an additional insured is strictly         The granting of primary status is contingent upon the existence
confined to the parameters outlined in the specific modifying        of a written contract requiring such an arrangement prior to the
form.                                                                loss.

Commonly, additional insured status is granted to project            Every insured, whether named or additional, has independent
owners, lessees, or general contractors who require protection       duties in the event of an incident, claim, or legal proceeding.
arising from the named insured operations.
                                                                     Immediate written notice of any event that may result in a claim
The scope of this external protection is generally limited to        must be provided to the administrative processing center.
vicarious liability stemming directly from the acts or omissions
of the named insured.                                                The failure of the named insured to provide notice does not
                                                                     excuse an additional insured from fulfilling their own reporting
Independent acts of negligence committed solely by the               obligations.
additional insured are routinely excluded from the scope of the
provided protection.                                                 All protected parties must cooperate fully in the investigation,
                                                                     settlement, or defense of the claim as requested by the claim
The separation of insureds provision ensures that the contract       administrators.
applies separately to each individual or entity claiming
protection.                                                          No insured may voluntarily make any payment, assume any
                                                                     obligation, or incur any expense without our prior written
This severability principle means that a breach of a condition by    authorization.
one insured does not automatically void the protection for
another innocent insured.                                            Any unauthorized financial commitments made by an insured
                                                                     will be their sole responsibility and will not be reimbursed.
Furthermore, the separation of insureds allows one protected
party to bring a valid claim against another protected party         The cancellation of the contract by the named insured
under the same contract.                                             immediately terminates the protection for all additional insureds
                                                                     simultaneously.
Despite this cross-liability application, the separation provision
does not multiply or increase the maximum limits of insurance        We are not obligated to provide separate notices of cancellation
available.                                                           to additional insureds unless explicitly mandated by a specific
                                                                     endorsement.
The Each Occurrence and applicable Aggregate limits remain
fixed, regardless of how many insured entities are implicated in     The rights and duties of the named insured cannot be
a single event.                                                      transferred to another party without our explicit written consent.

Additional insured endorsements often distinguish between            In the event of the named insured death or bankruptcy,
ongoing operations and the products-completed operations             temporary administrative rights may transfer to a legal
hazard.                                                              representative.

Protection for ongoing operations ceases the moment the
specific project is finished or the named insured departs the job
site.

documents.                                                     claim examiners.

and the language in an attached endorsement, the               exclusions and the overall scope of the liability contract.
endorsement takes precedence.
                                                               A material change in the risk profile, such as the introduction of
Exclusionary endorsements are specifically designed to         a new excluded hazard, can severely impact the availability of

to the situation.

contract.

For example, liabilities arising from the use of automobiles are  advisory organizations to address emerging legal precedents

POLICYHOLDER NOTICE - INFORMATION ABOUT YOUR POLICY
______________________________________________________________________________________

This notice describes our institutional information practices and     If we receive a valid subpoena or court order compelling the
outlines how we collect, use, and protect your commercial data.        production of your records, we will comply with the legal mandate
                                                                      accordingly.
We are committed to safeguarding the sensitive business and
personal information entrusted to us during the underwriting and      Premium auditors and loss control inspectors acting on our behalf
administration of your policy.                                        will receive only the specific data necessary to evaluate your
                                                                      premises and exposures.
The primary purpose of collecting this information is to evaluate
your risk profile, determine appropriate premium rates, and           You have the right to request access to the recorded personal and
process potential liability claims.                                   commercial information we have collected about your
                                                                      organization.
We obtain most of our data directly from you or your authorized
insurance broker through applications, supplementary                   To exercise this right, you must submit a formal written request to
questionnaires, and direct correspondence.                            our designated privacy officer at the mailing address provided in
                                                                      the declarations.
In addition to the information you provide, we may gather
supplementary data from external third-party sources to verify        Your written request must clearly identify the specific policy
your operational exposures.                                           numbers and the exact nature of the information you wish to
                                                                      review.
These external sources may include commercial credit reporting
agencies, loss history databases, public property records, and        We will acknowledge your request promptly and arrange for you to
governmental regulatory filings.                                      inspect and copy the requested records within thirty business
                                                                      days.
Information collected during the underwriting process may include
details about your business structure, operational territories,       We reserve the right to charge a reasonable administrative fee to
financial stability, and past litigation history.                      cover the costs associated with retrieving, copying, and mailing
                                                                      the requested documents.
We may also collect specific details regarding your physical
premises, safety protocols, employee training programs, and            If you believe that any information in our files is inaccurate,
quality control procedures.                                           incomplete, or irrelevant, you may request a formal correction or
                                                                      deletion.
Access to your sensitive commercial information is strictly
restricted to our internal employees, authorized affiliates, and      We will investigate your dispute and either make the requested
designated operational vendors.                                       amendments or notify you of our refusal to change the disputed
                                                                      record.
Our personnel are granted access to your data only to the extent
necessary to perform their specific job functions related to your     If we refuse to amend the record, you have the right to file a
coverage.                                                             concise statement detailing what you believe is the correct
                                                                      information.
We maintain robust physical, electronic, and procedural
safeguards designed to protect your information against               Your statement of dispute will be permanently appended to the
unauthorized access, accidental loss, or malicious disclosure.        relevant file and included in any future disclosures of the
                                                                      contested information.
Our cybersecurity protocols are regularly reviewed, updated, and
tested to ensure compliance with applicable state and federal data    This privacy notice is provided for your informational purposes
protection regulations.                                               only and does not alter, amend, or expand the specific coverage
                                                                      terms of your policy.
We do not sell your proprietary business information, customer
lists, or operational data to external marketing organizations under  We will provide an updated copy of this privacy notice annually, as
any circumstances.                                                    long as you maintain an active commercial insurance relationship
                                                                      with our organization.
We may disclose your information to third parties without your
prior written authorization only when explicitly permitted or         If our internal information practices change materially, we will
required by law.                                                      distribute a revised notice detailing the new procedures prior to
                                                                      their implementation.
Permitted disclosures include sharing information with
independent claims adjusters, legal counsel, and specialized         Please retain this document with your permanent insurance
investigators to facilitate the resolution of liability claims.       records for future reference regarding your data privacy rights and
                                                                      our institutional obligations.
We may also share relevant data with reinsurance companies to
secure adequate capacity for the limits of liability provided under
your policy.

Information may be disclosed to law enforcement agencies or
regulatory authorities to prevent suspected insurance fraud or
address other illegal activities.

The administrative framework of this contract relies upon your    5. You are expressly prohibited from taking any actions that
full cooperation to accurately assess the circumstances           might prejudice our ability to defend the claim or negotiate a
surrounding any reported incident.                                favorable settlement.

When requested by our claims personnel, you must promptly         Any intentional misrepresentation of facts, concealment of
provide access to all relevant organizational records,             evidence, or collusion with the claimant will result in the
documents, and electronic data.                                   immediate forfeiture of protection.

This includes, but is not limited to, employee training logs,     You must not enter into any agreements with third parties that
maintenance schedules, operational manuals, and internal          attempt to assign liability or alter the legal dynamics of the
incident investigation reports.                                   claim.

2. You must facilitate interviews between our investigators and  If you possess any contractual rights to seek indemnification or

possess relevant knowledge.                                       rights entirely.

or through virtual platforms, depending on the logistical         rights against third parties who may be responsible for the
requirements of the investigation.                                incident.

incident.                                                         recovery department.

statements.                                                       outlined elsewhere in this contract.

3. You must assist our representatives in securing physical       Your failure to maintain comprehensive operational records
evidence and identifying third-party witnesses who can            may hinder the defense process and complicate the resolution
corroborate your version of events.                               of the liability demand.

When requested, you must grant our investigators and retained     7. We expect your organization to maintain standard
experts unrestricted access to the physical premises where the    commercial documentation practices consistent with your
incident occurred.                                                specific industry classification and operational scope.

This access is necessary to conduct site inspections, take        If your lack of cooperation materially prejudices our ability to

defense services.                                                 increased the financial exposure.

case.                                                             for ongoing liability protection.

documents.                                                         claim examiners.

and the language in an attached endorsement, the                   exclusions and the overall scope of the liability contract.
endorsement takes precedence.

               LITIGATION MANAGEMENT AND DEFENSE ADMINISTRATION
______________________________________________________________________________________
THIS FORM IS PART OF THE POLICY AND MUST BE READ WITH THE DECLARATIONS AND ENDORSEMENTS.
______________________________________________________________________________________

1. Our organization assumes the exclusive authority to manage    In situations where a lawsuit contains both covered allegations
the legal response to any qualified liability demand presented    and allegations excluded by this contract, we will provide a
against your enterprise.                                         defense for the entire action.

This authority encompasses the complete direction of all         5. However, we reserve the right to issue a formal reservation
litigation strategies, settlement negotiations, and the selection   of rights regarding the specific allegations that fall outside the
of appropriate legal representation.                             coverage scope.

When a qualified legal action is initiated, we will appoint legal   This reservation of rights ensures that our provision of a
counsel to represent your interests in the pending judicial      defense does not constitute a waiver of our right to deny
proceedings.                                                     financial responsibility.

The selection of the defense attorney remains entirely within    We will not provide financial reimbursement for any judgments
our discretion, utilizing our network of approved legal          or settlements associated with the uncovered portions of the
professionals and specialized firms.                             legal action.

2. You may request the appointment of specific counsel;          You retain the option to hire independent legal counsel, at your
however, we have no obligation to honor such requests            own expense, to monitor the litigation and advise you on
unless mandated by jurisdiction.                                 uncovered exposures.

The appointed legal counsel will focus solely on defending the   6. Any independent counsel retained by your organization must
allegations that fall within the scope of this commercial liability  fully cooperate with the primary defense attorney appointed by
contract.                                                        our claims department.

We maintain the authority to investigate any claim or suit at our  The primary defense attorney retains ultimate control over the
discretion, utilizing internal personnel or independent         direction of the litigation and the presentation of the defense in
investigative resources.                                         court.

During the course of the litigation, we will determine the most  We will not reimburse any legal fees, consultation costs, or
appropriate legal strategy to mitigate potential financial      administrative expenses incurred by your independently
exposures.                                                       retained legal counsel.

3. We possess the unilateral authority to negotiate and finalize  If a conflict of interest arises that legally requires the
the settlement of any claim or suit without requiring your explicit appointment of independent defense counsel, we will fund such
consent.                                                         representation at prevailing rates.

Our settlement decisions are based on a comprehensive            7. The prevailing rates for independent counsel will be
evaluation of liability exposure, anticipated litigation costs, and  determined based on standard legal fees for similar litigation
jurisdictional venue factors.                                    within the specific geographic venue.

If we determine that a negotiated resolution is the most prudent  We require the independent counsel to adhere to our standard
course of action, we will execute the settlement on your behalf.  litigation management guidelines and billing protocols
                                                                 throughout the duration of the case.
Our obligation to provide legal representation ceases
immediately upon the exhaustion of the applicable limit          Any failure by the independent counsel to comply with these
scheduled in the policy declarations.                            administrative guidelines may result in the reduction or denial
                                                                 of fee reimbursements.
4. Once the relevant limit has been entirely depleted through
the payment of judgments or settlements, we will withdraw from   The administration of the defense process is designed to
the defense.                                                     protect both your organizational assets and our financial
                                                                 interests under this contract.
You will be formally notified in writing when the applicable limit
is approaching exhaustion and when it has been fully depleted.   8. We will keep your designated organizational representative

Following the depletion of the limit, the responsibility for funding

any ongoing legal representation transfers entirely to your
organization.                                                    Ultimately, the final determination regarding trial progression

      POLICYHOLDER NOTICE REGARDING CLAIM REPORTING AND LATE NOTICE
____________________________________________________________________________________________________

POLICYHOLDER NOTICE - INFORMATION ABOUT YOUR POLICY
____________________________________________________________________________________________________

A. This important policyholder notice outlines your strict       Failure to report an occurrence, claim, or suit promptly may result
obligations regarding the prompt reporting of occurrences,     in a complete denial of coverage for the delayed matter.
offenses, claims, and suits under this policy.                 We evaluate late notice situations based on whether the delay
Timely notification is a fundamental condition precedent to    materially prejudiced our ability to investigate the facts or mount a
coverage and is critical to our ability to investigate and defend  proper defense.
liability claims effectively.                                  Material prejudice occurs when critical evidence is lost, witnesses
You must notify us as soon as practicable of any occurrence or become unavailable, or the physical scene of the incident is
offense which may reasonably be expected to result in a liability substantially altered.
claim.                                                         We strongly recommend establishing internal corporate protocols
An occurrence includes any accident, continuous exposure to   to ensure that all frontline employees report incidents immediately
harmful conditions, or unexpected event that causes bodily injury  to your designated risk manager.
or property damage.                                            E. Your risk manager or designated representative should be

APPLICATION OF SCHEDULE LIMITS AND AGGREGATE DEPLETION


THIS FORM IS PART OF THE POLICY AND MUST BE READ WITH THE DECLARATIONS AND ENDORSEMENTS.


1. The numerical values displayed on the limits schedule represent the absolute maximum financial responsibility assumed by the carrier under this specific contract.

These scheduled maximums apply regardless of the number of protected entities, the number of individuals injured, or the number of claims filed.

The general aggregate limit establishes the maximum amount the carrier will disburse for all combined incidents occurring during the active policy period.

This general aggregate maximum encompasses all financial responsibilities except those specifically allocated to the products and completed operations hazard category.

2. As disbursements are made to resolve qualifying incidents, the remaining available balance of the general aggregate limit is correspondingly depleted.

Once the general aggregate limit is entirely exhausted by cumulative disbursements, the carrier holds no further obligation to respond to subsequent incidents.

The products and completed operations aggregate limit functions independently and establishes a separate maximum for incidents arising from distributed goods or finished work.

Disbursements allocated to the products and completed operations category do not reduce the available balance of the general aggregate limit.

3. The each occurrence limit defines the maximum financial responsibility for all damages arising out of a single, continuous, or repeated exposure event.

The each occurrence limit remains subject to the available remaining balance of the applicable aggregate limit at the time the incident is resolved.

If multiple scheduled locations are designated on the declarations, the general aggregate limit may be modified to apply separately to each distinct premises.

The separate application of the aggregate limit per location must be explicitly authorized by a designated endorsement attached to the policy documents.

4. The personal and advertising injury limit establishes the maximum disbursement available for all offenses committed against any single person or organization.

This specific limit is also subordinate to the general aggregate limit and will be restricted by any prior depletion of that overall maximum.

The medical expense limit provides a designated sub-limit for immediate medical costs incurred by third parties, regardless of established fault.

Disbursements made under the medical expense sub-limit are automatically deducted from the available balance of the each occurrence limit.

5. The damage to premises rented to you limit establishes a specific maximum for fire-related incidents occurring at leased commercial facilities.

This leased premises sub-limit applies strictly to the specific location where the enterprise maintains a formal lease agreement and conducts daily operations.

The scheduled limits apply exclusively to incidents that occur entirely within the designated coverage territory defined in the primary policy text.

Incidents occurring outside the designated territory will not be evaluated against the scheduled limits unless a specific international endorsement is attached.

6. The concept of severability of interests ensures that the scheduled limits apply separately to each protected entity facing a formal claim.

However, the application of severability does not increase the absolute maximum limits of insurance available for any single occurrence or aggregate period.

If a single incident triggers multiple sub-limits, the carrier will not disburse an amount exceeding the highest applicable single limit of insurance.

The enterprise cannot combine or stack the limits of multiple consecutive policy periods to resolve a single, continuous exposure event.

7. Continuous exposure events spanning multiple policy periods will be assigned exclusively to the single policy period where the damage first became evident.

The carrier will provide written notification to the first named insured when any aggregate limit has been depleted by more than fifty percent.

A final written notification will be issued immediately upon the complete exhaustion of any aggregate limit scheduled on the declarations page.

Any supplementary payments or administrative expenses incurred by the carrier during the resolution process do not reduce the scheduled limits of insurance.

8. The limits of insurance will automatically reset to their full scheduled value at the inception of each new annual renewal period.

Modifications to the scheduled limits requested mid-term will apply only to incidents occurring after the effective date of the approved change endorsement.

declarations.                                                   cancellation notices or policy changes to any other scheduled
                                                                insured parties.

                                                                We maintain the right to conduct a comprehensive risk control
                                                                survey of the new entity before finalizing any transfer of rights.

                                                                Failure to disclose material changes in operations during a
                                                                transfer request constitutes grounds for immediate rescission of
                                                                the transfer endorsement.

scheduled operations.                                            phrase is specifically defined within the policy definitions

will generally control.                                          forms, and endorsements immediately upon receipt to ensure

determination of the claim.                                      not automatically grant coverage if another unamended

territory 007 only when the declarations show the same exposure basis.

SECTION 286 - AGGREGATE LIMIT APPLICATION
For class 47103 (Printing operations) at Location 6, with Silica or Silica-
Related Dust Exclusion, the applicable form is CG 20 10 edition 09 21 and
the provision is treated as condition.

The Medical Expense limit of $5,000 applies with the Commercial General
Liability coverage part for Location 6, class 47103, territory 007, rated on
payroll of 1,047,270, and does not increase another aggregate.

SECTION 287 - ADDITIONAL INSURED CONTRACT GATE
6. The provision below is read with CG 20 10 edition 09 21 for Location 6,
class 47103, territory 007.

Additional insured status for Location 6, class 47103, territory 007 applies
only when the contract requirement and attached form CG 20 10 edition 09
21 are both satisfied; the Silica or Silica-Related Dust Exclusion provision
remains applicable.

SECTION 288 - EXCLUSION AND ENDORSEMENT PRIORITY
CG 20 10 edition 09 21 is a exclusion provision for Location 6, class 47103,
territory 007.

The Silica or Silica-Related Dust Exclusion provision and form CG 20 10
edition 09 21 control before any conflicting summary entry for Location 6,
class 47103, territory 007.

                     LITIGATION MANAGEMENT AND DEFENSE ADMINISTRATION

____________________________________________________________________________________________________
THIS FORM IS PART OF THE POLICY AND MUST BE READ WITH THE DECLARATIONS AND ENDORSEMENTS.
____________________________________________________________________________________________________

Our organization assumes the exclusive authority to manage     In situations where a lawsuit contains both covered allegations
the legal response to any qualified liability demand presented     and allegations excluded by this contract, we will provide a
against your enterprise.                                           defense for the entire action.

This authority encompasses the complete direction of all         However, we reserve the right to issue a formal reservation of
litigation strategies, settlement negotiations, and the selection   rights regarding the specific allegations that fall outside the
of appropriate legal representation.                               coverage scope.

When a qualified legal action is initiated, we will appoint legal    This reservation of rights ensures that our provision of a
counsel to represent your interests in the pending judicial         defense does not constitute a waiver of our right to deny
proceedings.                                                       financial responsibility.

The selection of the defense attorney remains entirely within      We will not provide financial reimbursement for any judgments
our discretion, utilizing our network of approved legal            or settlements associated with the uncovered portions of the
professionals and specialized firms.                               legal action.

You may request the appointment of specific counsel; however,      You retain the option to hire independent legal counsel, at your
we are under no obligation to honor such requests unless           own expense, to monitor the litigation and advise you on
mandated by jurisdiction.                                          uncovered exposures.

The appointed legal counsel will focus solely on defending the     Any independent counsel retained by your organization must
allegations that fall within the scope of this commercial liability  fully cooperate with the primary defense attorney appointed by
contract.                                                          our claims department.

We maintain the authority to investigate any claim or suit at our    The primary defense attorney retains ultimate control over the
discretion, utilizing internal personnel or independent            direction of the litigation and the presentation of the defense in
investigative resources.                                           court.

During the course of the litigation, we will determine the most    We will not reimburse any legal fees, consultation costs, or
appropriate legal strategy to mitigate potential financial          administrative expenses incurred by your independently
exposures.                                                         retained legal counsel.

We possess the unilateral authority to negotiate and finalize the     If a conflict of interest arises that legally requires the
settlement of any claim or suit without requiring your explicit    appointment of independent defense counsel, we will fund such
consent.                                                           representation at prevailing rates.

Our settlement decisions are based on a comprehensive              The prevailing rates for independent counsel will be determined
evaluation of liability exposure, anticipated litigation costs, and   based on standard legal fees for similar litigation within the
jurisdictional venue factors.                                      specific geographic venue.

If we determine that a negotiated resolution is the most prudent   We require the independent counsel to adhere to our standard
course of action, we will execute the settlement on your behalf.   litigation management guidelines and billing protocols

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

                    SILICA OR SILICA-RELATED DUST EXCLUSION

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
THIS FORM IS PART OF THE POLICY AND MUST BE READ WITH THE DECLARATIONS AND ENDORSEMENTS.
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

EFFECTIVE DATE 02/20/2026                        CHANGE CLASSIFICATION Material
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
CLASS / TERRITORY 41670 / 007                    LOCATION 2
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
LIMIT General Aggregate: $2,000,000              FORM CG 20 10 04 13
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

A. Classification And Exposure Reference

This form applies to Restaurants - with sales of alcoholic beverages
at Location 2, territory 007, using class code 41670.

The rating schedule shows gross sales of 107,692, a general
aggregate limit of $2,000,000, and premium $5,546.

This endorsement addresses Silica or Silica-Related Dust
Exclusion under form CG 20 10 edition 04 13.

This endorsement modifies the commercial general liability
coverage part and establishes an absolute exclusion for exposures
related to silica and silica-related dust.

B. The provisions detailed in this document apply to all liability
coverages, classifications, locations, and operations scheduled on
the issued policy.

Coverage does not apply to any bodily injury or property damage
arising out of the actual, alleged, or threatened presence of silica.

The exclusion equally applies to personal and advertising injury
claims stemming from the distribution, sale, handling, or inhalation
of such materials.

For the purposes of this endorsement, silica is defined as silicon
dioxide occurring in crystalline, amorphous, or impure forms,
including sand and quartz.

Silica-related dust is defined as a mixture or combination of silica
and other dust particles that may become airborne during business
operations.

C. The carrier bears no obligation to provide indemnification for any
loss, cost, settlement, or expense related to the specified mineral
compounds.

Furthermore, the carrier assumes no responsibility to defend any
suit, action, or proceeding seeking damages attributable to silica or
silica-related dust.

The restriction extends to any discharge, dispersal, seepage,
migration, release, or escape of the dust into the environment or
indoor workspaces.

Coverage is excluded whether the introduction of the dust was
sudden, accidental, gradual, or occurred over an extended period
of time.

No coverage is provided for any request, demand, order, or
statutory requirement that any insured or others test for or monitor
the dust.

D. Similarly, costs associated with cleaning up, removing,
containing, treating, detoxifying, or neutralizing the specified
mineral dust are entirely excluded from this policy.

Claims made by or on behalf of any governmental authority for
damages resulting from testing, monitoring, or remediation are also
excluded.

Any product, material, or good manufactured, sold, handled,
distributed, or disposed of by the insured containing these minerals
falls under this restriction.

Liability assumed under any contract or agreement regarding the
remediation or containment of these dust particles is similarly
excluded from coverage.

This endorsement supersedes any other provision, endorsement,
or exception that might otherwise grant coverage for environmental,
occupational, or pollution-related exposures.

E. The restriction applies to operations conducted at scheduled
premises, temporary worksites, and all products and completed
operations hazards involving the specified dust.

If any portion of a claim involves allegations both related and
unrelated to the excluded dust, the carrier will not allocate defense
costs.

Instead, the entire claim shall be deemed excluded if the primary or
underlying allegation stems from the presence of the specified
minerals.

Insureds are expected to maintain accurate records of materials
used in their manufacturing, construction, or contracting processes
to verify compliance.

Failure on the part of the insured to identify the presence of these
minerals in raw materials does not invalidate this exclusion.

F. The carrier reserves the right to deny indemnification for any
settlement reached without prior written consent regarding these
specific mineral liabilities.

This exclusion applies to all exposure bases, including gross sales,
payroll, area, and cost of work, regardless of premium calculation
methods.

Any exception to pollution exclusions found elsewhere in the policy
documentation does not apply to the mineral compounds defined
herein.

The provisions set forth in this endorsement are absolute and apply
to all operations, classifications, and territories associated with the
insured business.

In the event that any court or jurisdiction finds a portion of this
exclusion unenforceable, the remaining provisions shall remain in
full effect.

G. Damages encompass statutory fines, penalties, punitive
assessments, and multiplied damages levied by governmental
bodies or regulatory agencies concerning the excluded dust.

The exclusion applies regardless of whether the dust was
introduced into the environment by the named insured or by any
third party.

No coverage exceptions apply for the completed operations hazard
or the products hazard when the underlying injury involves the
specified mineral compounds.

This endorsement controls over any conflicting provisions in the
coverage part and applies consistently across all scheduled limits
and classifications.

____________________________________________________________________________________________________

                     DESIGNATED PROFESSIONAL SERVICES EXCLUSION
____________________________________________________________________________________________________

THIS FORM IS PART OF THE POLICY AND MUST BE READ WITH THE DECLARATIONS AND ENDORSEMENTS.
____________________________________________________________________________________________________

EFFECTIVE DATE 05/20/2026                            CHANGE CLASSIFICATION Potentially Material
........................................................................................................................................................................
CLASS / TERRITORY 97047 / 012                        LOCATION 5
........................................................................................................................................................................
LIMIT Damage to Premises Rented to You: $100,000       FORM CG 21 67 04 13
........................................................................................................................................................................

A. Classification And Exposure Reference

This form applies to Property owners - commercial buildings at
Location 5, territory 012, using class code 97047.

The rating schedule shows area of 130,133, a damage to premises
rented to you limit of $100,000, and premium $1,457.

This endorsement addresses Designated Professional Services
Exclusion under form CG 21 67 edition 04 13.

This endorsement modifies the commercial general liability
coverage part and applies to the specific operations or
classifications designated in the accompanying schedules.

B. The provisions herein restrict the scope of coverage available for
certain specialized activities.

No coverage is afforded for bodily injury or property damage
originating from the performance or omission of any professional
service.

This restriction applies equally to personal and advertising injury
originating from the same performance or omission of professional
duties.

The term professional service encompasses any activity requiring
specialized knowledge, advanced training, or licensed expertise in
a specific field of practice.

Examples of such restricted activities include the preparation or
approval of maps, shop drawings, opinions, reports, or surveys.

C. Supervisory, inspection, architectural, or engineering activities
are strictly excluded from the liability framework provided by this
coverage part.

Medical, surgical, dental, x-ray, or nursing services fall entirely
outside the scope of protection.

Any instructional, educational, or consulting services provided by
the named insured or on the named insured's behalf are similarly
restricted.

The exclusion operates regardless of whether the professional
service is a primary component of the business operations or an
incidental activity.

Claims alleging negligent hiring, employment, training, or
supervision of individuals performing these restricted services will
not trigger the defense or indemnity provisions.

D. If a claim involves both ordinary negligence and professional
negligence, the entire claim shall be excluded if the ordinary
negligence is intertwined with the professional service.

The carrier assumes no obligation to investigate, settle, or defend
any suit or demand that involves allegations rooted in the
designated professional services.

Costs and attorney fees incurred in responding to such allegations
must be borne solely by the named insured.

This restriction applies to any individual or organization qualifying
as an insured under the liability framework, including employees,
volunteer workers, and executive officers.

When the designated professional services are performed by
independent contractors or subcontractors on behalf of the named
insured, the exclusion remains fully applicable.

E. The classification code and exposure basis shown in the rating
schedule do not override or negate the application of this
professional services restriction.

Even if a premium charge is developed based on gross sales or
payroll associated with the professional activity, the liability
exclusion remains absolute.

No exception is granted for bodily injury occurring on the described
premises if the proximate cause is the rendering of the specialized
service.

The products-completed operations hazard does not encompass
any injury or damage resulting from the failure of the professional
service to meet expected standards.

Any warranties or representations made regarding the quality,
fitness, or performance of the professional service are excluded
from the scope of the liability framework.

F. Data privacy violations, unauthorized access to confidential
information, and similar cyber events arising during the professional
service are not addressed by this endorsement.

The carrier reserves the right to withdraw from the defense of any
litigation upon determining the facts fall within this restriction.

Notice of such withdrawal will be provided to the named insured in
accordance with the administrative conditions governing
communication and correspondence.

The named insured is responsible for maintaining separate
professional liability or errors and omissions coverage to address
the exposures excluded by this endorsement.

The existence or absence of such separate professional liability
coverage has no bearing on the interpretation or enforcement of
this specific exclusion.

G. In the event of a dispute regarding the classification of an activity
as a professional service, the customary standards of the relevant
industry will be considered.

However, the final determination of whether an activity constitutes a
professional service under this policy rests upon the definitions and
restrictions outlined herein.

The application of this endorsement supersedes any conflicting
language found in the primary liability coverage forms or previously
issued amendatory documents.

The remaining provisions, limits, and conditions of the commercial
general liability coverage part continue in full force and effect
without alteration.
